              if (t) parts.push(t);\n                }\n            });\n            return parts.join(' ').trim();\n        } catch (_) { return ''; }\n    }\n\n    function getVisibleText(el) {\n         if (!node.textContent || !node.textContent.trim()) {\n                            return NodeFilter.FILTER_REJECT;\n                        }\n                        const parent =                 return 'img';\n                case 'ul':\n                case 'ol':\n                    return 'list';\n                case 'li':\n                    return 'listitem';\n
